The service and Frozen yogurt are great. The staff was very friendly and helpful. Said hi as soon as we walked in and asked if we needed help, but did not but us when we said no. Great staff. < Text>
The church offers reverance and devotion in the sacrifice of the Latin Mass.  It's not a simple matter of the mass in Latin.  The entire atmosphere is soaked in hundreds of years of tradition and respectful adoration.  If you take the time to learn the Latin you understand that the English versions of the mass (which are called celebrations and not sacrifice) since Vatican II are not at all the same.  There is much to be gained in the prayer and reverance of the traditional mass.<//Text>

<Text>I was baptized at birth (I'm approaching 24 now), and my thoughts on faith, spirituality, god, what have you... Have gone on an interesting journey to say the least. While I still don't at present consider myself a Catholic or a Christian even (or maybe even a theist in the traditional sense of God watching over us and caring for us and guiding us and all that), I have tremendous respect for those with a deep faith in the unknown.

It was following the death of an old family friend, Fr. Francisco Vincente, O.P., that I found myself drawn to Gregorian Chant. This past weekend, while walking the beach listening to Paschale Mysterium, I decided I'd find a Latin Mass. I came to the Sun. 11:30 Mass. It's been a long time since I've been to church that wasn't out of desperation, or to pay respect to the dead, or to fulfill familial duties. And I've never been to a Latin Mass. But I really enjoyed the experience, and I look forward to going again. The pastor gave a tremendous homily too.

EDIT 7/28/18: After sporadically attending Mass (Tridentine of course!) A few more times, I finally began regularly attending starting Easter. In June I moved back out to East Bay, but still try to make it out to Star at least once a month -- the building, the reverence, the priests all hold a special place in my heart.< /Text>< Gmap_id>

<rating>3<//rating><review>I wish there was an option to give 3.5 stars on Google because I would for Burger House. The only reason I'm not giving them 4 stars is that the shake I had was not good, the garlic fries were incredibly oily, and the food is expensive for what it is. That said, the Cheese burger was excellent and the service was pretty quick. I came in on a pre-Christmas Friday night and the streets were filled with Christmas shoppers and tourists. Her Peking beef is made with tender beef that just melts in your mouth. And Her Egg Flower soup is the Best in Sacramento!!! One other thing I must mention. We celebrated my husband's 50th birthday here and we were so happy that we did.</text>
